<script>
    window.feedbackUri = '/feedback';
    window.feedbackParams = [];
    window.feedbackReady = false;

    window.feedbackCallbacks = window.feedbackCallbacks || [];

    window.distinctId = 'BADB1039-8590-4A88-B3DB-443E6587DC07';
    function addToResult(result, add) {
        result = result || {};
        add = add || {};
        for(var k in add){
            if(add.hasOwnProperty(k)){
                result[k]=add[k];
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

    (function(window, $) {
        initFeedback(window.distinctId);

        window.Feedback = window.Feedback || {};
        window.Feedback.update = function(additionalParams, callback) {
            additionalParams = additionalParams || {};
            var distinct_id = window.distinctId || false;
            var feedbackUri = window.feedbackUri || false;
            if(feedbackUri) {
                if(distinct_id) {
                    if(feedbackUri.indexOf('?')!==-1) {
                        feedbackUri += '&';
                    }
                    else {
                        feedbackUri += '?';
                    }
                    feedbackUri += 'distinct_id='+distinct_id;
                }
            }
            console.log("Feedback.update: ",feedbackUri);
            updateFeedback(feedbackUri, additionalParams, callback);
        };
        window.Feedback.fetch = function(callback) {
            var distinct_id = window.distinctId || false;
            var feedbackUri = window.feedbackUri || false;
            if(feedbackUri) {
                if(distinct_id) {
                    if(feedbackUri.indexOf('?')!==-1) {
                        feedbackUri += '&';
                    }
                    else {
                        feedbackUri += '?';
                    }
                    feedbackUri += 'distinct_id='+distinct_id;
                }
            }
            console.log("Feedback.update: ",feedbackUri);
            updateFeedback(feedbackUri, callback);
        };

        // add feedback to elastic
        window.Feedback.pushToElastic = function (params) {
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push(params);
        };

        function initFeedback(distinct_id) {
            distinct_id = distinct_id || false;
            var feedbackUri = window.feedbackUri;
            if(distinct_id) {
                if(feedbackUri.indexOf('?')!==-1) {
                    feedbackUri += '&';
                }
                else {
                    feedbackUri += '?';
                }
                feedbackUri += 'distinct_id='+distinct_id;
            }
            //console.log("initFeedback: ",feedbackUri);
            //create/update feedback id
            updateFeedback(feedbackUri);
        }
        function updateFeedback(feedbackUri, params, callback) {
            //console.log("updateFeedback: ",feedbackUri);
            callback = callback || function(clickId) {};
            if(!feedbackUri || !feedbackUri.length) {
                callback.call(this,[null]);
                return false;
            }
            params = params || {};
            //console.log("params: ",params);
            params['language'] = window.locale;
            params = addToResult(params, window.feedbackParams);
            // if(additionalParams) {
            //     var params = [];
            //     for(var i in additionalParams) {
            //         params.push(encodeURIComponent(i)+'='+encodeURIComponent(additionalParams[i]));
            //     }
            //     if(params && params.length) {
            //         if(feedbackUri.indexOf('?')!==-1) {
            //             feedbackUri += '&';
            //         }
            //         else {
            //             feedbackUri += '?';
            //         }
            //         feedbackUri += params.join('&');
            //     }
            // }
            //create/update feedback id
            $(function() {
                $.ajax({
                    method: 'POST',
                    url: feedbackUri,
                    data: params,
                    cache: false,
                    withCredentials: true,
                    timeout: 30000, // sets timeout to 3 seconds
                    success: function(data) {
                        console.log("initFeedback: ",data);
                        if(data && data.hasOwnProperty('clickId')) {
                            window.clickId = data.clickId;

                            // if(data.clickData && data.clickData.distinct_id && window.mixpanel) {
                            //     window.mixpanel.identify(data.clickData.distinct_id);
                            // }

                            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
                            window.dataLayer.push({
                                event: 'feedback_init',
                                clickId: data.clickId,
                                clickData: data.clickData || {}
                            });
                        }
                        window.feedbackReady = true;

                        for (var i = 0; i < window.feedbackCallbacks.length; ++i) {
                            try {
                                window.feedbackCallbacks[i](data.clickId, data.clickData);
                            } catch (err) {}
                        }
                        callback.call(this,[data.clickId, data.clickData]);
                    },
                    error: function(error) {
                        console.log("initFeedback: ",error);
                        window.feedbackReady = true;

                        for (var i = 0; i < window.feedbackCallbacks.length; ++i) {
                            try {
                                window.feedbackCallbacks[i](false);
                            } catch (err) {}
                        }
                        callback.call(this,[null]);
                    }
                });
            });
        }
        function fetchFeedback(feedbackUri, callback) {
            console.log("fetchFeedback: ",feedbackUri);
            callback = callback || function(clickId) {};
            if(!feedbackUri || !feedbackUri.length) {
                callback.call(this,[null]);
                return false;
            }
            //create/update feedback id
            $(function() {
                $.ajax({
                    method: 'get',
                    url: feedbackUri,
                    data: {},
                    cache: false,
                    withCredentials: true,
                    timeout: 3000, // sets timeout to 3 seconds
                    success: function(data) {
                        console.log("fetchFeedback: ",data);
                        if(data && data.hasOwnProperty('clickId')) {
                            window.clickId = data.clickId;
                        }
                        callback.call(this,[data.clickId]);
                    },
                    error: function(error) {
                        console.log("fetchFeedback: ",error);
                        callback.call(this,[null]);
                    }
                });
            });
        }
    })(window, $);
</script>

<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 mb-16px mb-last-0">Our headquarters are in the European country of Romania. With its strong privacy laws, Romania is not part of any international surveillance alliance. We are not legally required to keep tabs on your digital identity.</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 mb-16px mb-last-0">Want to know more about how we handle any requests for data? (Spoiler alert: We comply but we have no data to show.) <a class='font-bold text-darkblue-30 hover-text-yellow-30' href='/en_US/transparency-report'>Check out our latest Transparancy Report</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>

Can’t <em class='font-normal text-highlight-yellow-15'>Choose</em>? </h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class='vb-paragraphs container'>
<div class='maxw-750px mx-auto last-child-paragraph-no-mb'>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 mb-16px mb-last-0 text-center">Whether you’re looking to download, stream, or game we have a server optimized for you. We’re <a class='font-bold text-darkblue-30 hover-text-yellow-30' href='/en_US/support'>available 24/7</a> to help you figure out which server is best for your needs.</p>

<div class="vb-text mb-18px sm-mb-36px">
<div class="px-16px">
<h2 class="text-darkblue-30 text-size-3 sm-text-size-2 font-bold text-left sm-text-center">
Inside CyberGhost’s <em class='font-normal text-highlight-yellow-15'>VPN Servers</em> </h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class='vb-paragraphs container'>
<div class='maxw-750px mx-auto last-child-paragraph-no-mb'>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">Your privacy and security mean everything to us. And that means ensuring our servers not just work, but protect you as well. Every single server is fully encrypted. If someone takes our server, <b>they won’t be able to disclose any information</b>. We use a combination of encryption and keys to hide all your information in plain sight.</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">But even if servers are taken, there is no information to be taken. We have an additional level of protection. <b>CyberGhost VPN's servers are RAM-only</b>. What does this mean? Rather than hard disks, all data is stored using volatile memory. If someone were to come into the facility where the servers are physically located, such as government agencies or spies, and try to take the servers out, they will encounter quite a problem. <b>Once a server is unplugged, all the data stored on the server will be completely erased. Everything is lost</b>.</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">With RAM servers, our customers are guaranteed extra security as unauthorized parties are unable to access the data, added layers of security that back our no-logs policy, and overall improved performance.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="vb-quote-section my-18px sm-my-36px">
<div class="vb-quote">
<div class="vb-quote_container container">
<div class="vb-quote_illustration">
<img class="" src="/img/vb/pages/vpn-server/quote.svg" alt="CyberGhost VPN">
</div>
<div class="vb-quote_content">
<div class="vb-quote_text ">
<p>"Our servers run on RAM-only; they are fully encrypted and have no ties to our databases or management infrastructure. Every reboot wipes them down, and even if they’re removed for the rack, they’re completely useless and can’t be accessed."</p>
</div>
<div class="vb-quote_author">
<div class="vb-quote_author_name">Tudor Fulga</div>
<div class="vb-quote_author_function">Head of Infrastructure, CyberGhost VPN</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class='vb-paragraphs container'>
<div class='maxw-750px mx-auto last-child-paragraph-no-mb'>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">On top of this, many of our servers are colocated. Colocated servers give us an additional advantage – <b>we own our own servers and, therefore, do not rent the hardware</b>. We are the only ones with remove access to these servers, which increases your security. Furthermore, because we own the devices, we can set them up for optimized peering connectivity.</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0"><b>We have colocated servers around the globe, including major cities like New York, London, and Paris.</b></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class='vb-spacing mt-60px sm-mt-80px'></div>
<div class="vb-text mb-18px sm-mb-36px">
<div class="px-16px">
<h2 class="text-darkblue-30 text-size-3 sm-text-size-2 font-bold text-left sm-text-center">
We Don’t Keep Any <em class='font-normal text-highlight-yellow-15'>Logs</em> </h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class='vb-paragraphs container'>
<div class='maxw-750px mx-auto last-child-paragraph-no-mb'>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">Our data retention stance has been clear from day one. What you do behind our encrypted connection isn’t any of our business.</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">In 2022, Deloitte, an independent auditing firm, inspected the integrity of our No Logs policy. The results confirmed our claims and continued commitment to privacy. (You can read the full report <a href='https://s3.eu-west-1.amazonaws.com/assets.cyberghostvpn.com/files/cg/CyberGhost+-+Independent+Limited+Assurance+Report.pdf'>here</a>.)</p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">As a result, you can rest assured we don’t log anything related to your incoming and outgoing traffic information. This includes user and destination IP addresses, browsing history, amount of data transferred, VPN servers used, and DNS queries or files downloaded. </p>
<p class="text-darkgray-20 text-size-7 text-left sm-text-center mb-16px mb-last-0">We don’t keep any data related to your VPN session either, including the software used, connection date, or duration.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div class="maxw-924px mx-auto">
<h2 class="text-darkblue-30 text-size-3 sm-text-size-2 font-bold text-center">
<em class='font-normal text-highlight-yellow-15'>FAQ</em>? </h2>
</div>
</div>
<section class="vb-questions tabs-requirements container-fluid ">
<div class="row">
<div class='container'>
<div class='maxw-924 mx-auto'>
<div class="panel-group accordion-questions-control" id='accordion-questions' role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">
<div class="panel panel-default">
<div class="panel-heading expanded" role="tab" id="heading-0">
<h4 class="panel-title">
<a role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-questions" href="#collapse-0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse-0">
<div class='display-table'>
 <div class='table-cell cell-control'>
<i class="fa fa-plus fa-fw"></i><i class="fa fa-minus fa-fw"></i>
</div>
<div class='table-cell cell-content content-title'>
What Is a VPN Server? </div>
</div>
</a>
</h4>
</div>
<div id="collapse-0" class="panel-collapse collapse  in" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="heading-0">
<div class="panel-body">
A VPN (virtual private network) server manages web traffic securely. VPN servers are physical or virtual machines that act as an intermediary between you and the internet. Most VPN servers have <a href='/en_US/transparency-report/fleet'>special hardware and software configurations</a> that help them better handle encrypted data transfers. Many of them don’t even have data storage devices. Some services, like CyberGhost VPN, have special servers for different kinds of traffic like <a href='/en_US/unblock-streaming'>streaming</a>, <a href='/en_US/vpn-torrent'>torrenting</a>, and so on. </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel panel-default">
<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="heading-1">
<h4 class="panel-title">
<a role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-questions" href="#collapse-1" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse-1">
<div class='display-table'>
<div class='table-cell cell-control'>
<i class="fa fa-plus fa-fw"></i><i class="fa fa-minus fa-fw"></i>
</div>
<div class='table-cell cell-content content-title'>
How Do I Change My VPN Server? </div>
</div>
</a>
</h4>
</div>
<div id="collapse-1" class="panel-collapse collapse " role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="heading-1">
<div class="panel-body">
It depends on the VPN you’re using. With CyberGhost VPN, changing your VPN server is easy. Just open the app, click on “Best server location” under the power button, and select “More servers.” You’ll come to the <a href='/en_US/vpn-server'>complete list of available servers</a> to select whichever you want. </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel panel-default">
<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="heading-2">
<h4 class="panel-title">
<a role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-questions" href="#collapse-2" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse-2">
<div class='display-table'>
<div class='table-cell cell-control'>
<i class="fa fa-plus fa-fw"></i><i class="fa fa-minus fa-fw"></i>
</div>
<div class='table-cell cell-content content-title'>
How Do I Choose a VPN Server? </div>
</div>
</a>
</h4>
</div>
<div id="collapse-2" class="panel-collapse collapse " role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="heading-2">
<div class="panel-body">
The best VPN tunnels are established with the servers that are closest to your location. The shorter the distance between you and the VPN server, the better the connection. If you just want to <a href='/en_US/advantages/hide-ip'>stay anonymous</a>, it’s best to choose a nearby VPN server. Sometimes, servers farther away can be better if the closer ones are really busy. Many VPN services also have specialty servers. Whether you want to stream, torrent, or <a href='/en_US/advantages/hide-ip'>play games online</a>, CyberGhost VPN has servers optimized for each of these. </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel panel-default">
<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="heading-3">
<h4 class="panel-title">
<a role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-questions" href="#collapse-3" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse-3">
<div class='display-table'>
<div class='table-cell cell-control'>
<i class="fa fa-plus fa-fw"></i><i class="fa fa-minus fa-fw"></i>
</div>
<div class='table-cell cell-content content-title'>
Are VPNs Legal? </div>
</div>
</a>
</h4>
</div>
<div id="collapse-3" class="panel-collapse collapse " role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="heading-3">
<div class="panel-body">
VPNs are legal in most places, but some countries outright <a href='/en_US/anti-censorship'>ban them</a>. Russia, Iraq, and Belarus have banned VPNs, while a handful of others, like China, UAE, and Iran strictly regulate VPN usage. Most countries don’t restrict or punish the use of VPNs. That said, laws change all the time, so we always recommend you double check local laws. You can use CyberGhost VPN servers even in countries where VPNs are illegal. </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel panel-default">
<div class="panel-heading" role="tab" id="heading-4">
<h4 class="panel-title">
<a role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-parent="#accordion-questions" href="#collapse-4" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="collapse-4">
<div class='display-table'>
<div class='table-cell cell-control'>
<i class="fa fa-plus fa-fw"></i><i class="fa fa-minus fa-fw"></i>
</div>
<div class='table-cell cell-content content-title'>
Why Don’t Free VPNs Have a Lot of Server Locations? </div>
</div>
</a>
</h4>
</div>
<div id="collapse-4" class="panel-collapse collapse " role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="heading-4">
<div class="panel-body">
Free VPNs don’t have many server locations because it’s expensive. Maintaining a global server network requires heavy infrastructure, personnel, and other costs. Instead of paying for upkeep on a quality network, many free VPNs provide just a few low quality servers using a freemium business model. That means the free provider sells your personal information to third parties in exchange for giving you “free” access. Paid VPNs like CyberGhost VPN focus on quality and quantity. You get access to a <a href='/en_US/buy'>global network of premium VPN servers</a> and can rest assured your data is completely safe. </div>
</div>
</div>
</div> 
</div> 
</div> 
</div>
